                        }

                            reject;
                        }
                    }

                    }
                }

                    term icmp {
                        from {
                            protocol icmp;
                        }
                        then policer icmpservice;
                    }
                    term final {
                        then policer u-homesave;
                    }
                }
            }

inactive: event-options {
    policy disable_ifd_mq_xm_ea_mpcs {
        events PIC;
        within 3 {
            trigger on 1;
        }
        attributes-match {
            PIC.message matches "FI: Cell un.*t [4-6][0-9]{4}|EPM[0-1]:.*eQ empty|EPM[0-1]:.*free pool single po|DDRIF: Ch.*m .*sum Errors 255|DRD[0-1]: Command seq.* err|DRD[0-1]*: .+ timeout error|FO: Cell pack|CPQ1: Queue un";
        }
        then {
            event-script disable_ifd_mq_xm_ea_mpcs.slax {
                arguments {
                    message "{$$.message}";
                }
            }
        }
    }
    policy disable_ifd_mq_xm_ea_mpcs_misc {
        events PIC;
        within 3 {
            trigger on 1;
        }
        attributes-match {
            PIC.message matches "Link sanity ch|BACK WEDGE DE|LUCHIP.* ucode data err|DDRIF FO[0-1] Checksum Error|Error .* module: PRECL.*, type:";
        }
        then {
            event-script disable_ifd_mq_xm_ea_mpcs.slax {
                arguments {
                    message "{$$.message}";
                }
            }
        }
    }
    event-script {
        file disable_ifd_mq_xm_ea_mpcs.slax;
        file Optic.slax;
    }
}

class-of-service {
    classifiers {
        dscp CL_DSCP {
            forwarding-class CS6 {
                loss-priority low code-points DSCP-48;
            }
            forwarding-class EF {
                loss-priority low code-points DSCP-46;
            }
        }
        dscp-ipv6 CL_IPV6_DSCP {
            forwarding-class CS6 {
                loss-priority low code-points [ DSCP-IPV6-46 DSCP-IPV6-48 ];
            }
            forwarding-class AF2 {
                loss-priority low code-points [ DSCP-IPV6-26 DSCP-IPV6-28 ];
            }
        }
        exp CL_EXP {
            forwarding-class CS6 {
                loss-priority low code-points 110;
            }
            forwarding-class EF {
                loss-priority low code-points 101;
            }
            forwarding-class AF4 {
                loss-priority low code-points 100;
            }
            forwarding-class AF3 {
                loss-priority low code-points 011;
            }
            forwarding-class AF2 {
                loss-priority low code-points 010;
            }
            forwarding-class AF1 {
                loss-priority low code-points 001;
            }
            forwarding-class BE {
                loss-priority low code-points 000;
            }
        }
    }
    code-point-aliases {
        dscp {
            DSCP-46 101110;
            DSCP-48 110000;
        }
        dscp-ipv6 {
            DSCP-IPV6-46 101110;
            DSCP-IPV6-48 110000;
            DSCP-IPV6-26 011010;
            DSCP-IPV6-28 011100;
        }
    }
    host-outbound-traffic {
        forwarding-class CS6;
        dscp-code-point cs6;
    }
    drop-profiles {
        BE_DROP_PROFILE {
            fill-level 100 drop-probability 100;
            fill-level 60 drop-probability 0;
        }
    }
    forwarding-classes {
        class CS7 queue-num 7;
        class AF3 queue-num 5;
        class AF2 queue-num 4;
        class AF4 queue-num 6;
        class CS6 queue-num 3;
        class EF queue-num 2;
        class AF1 queue-num 1;
        class BE queue-num 0;
    }
    interfaces {
        ge-1/1/1 {
            unit * {
                classifiers {
                    dscp-ipv6 CL_IPV6_DSCP;
                }
            }
            /* VOD -> EF */
            unit 36 {
                forwarding-class EF;
            }
            /* 3G-IPv4 -> EF */
            unit 200 {
                forwarding-class CS6;
            }
            /* 4G-IPv4-> EF */
            unit 300 {
                forwarding-class EF;
            }
            /* 4G-IPv6 -> EF */
            unit 306 {
                forwarding-class EF;
            }
        }
        ae0 {
            scheduler-map SCH_MAP;
            unit * {
                classifiers {
                    dscp CL_DSCP;
                    exp CL_EXP;
                }
                rewrite-rules {
                    dscp RW_DSCP;
                    exp RW_EXP;
                }
            }
        }
        ae1 {
            scheduler-map SCH_MAP;
            unit * {
                classifiers {
                    dscp CL_DSCP;
                    exp CL_EXP;
                }
                rewrite-rules {
                    dscp RW_DSCP;
                    exp RW_EXP;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    routing-instances {
        all {
            classifiers {
                exp CL_EXP;
            }
        }
    }
    rewrite-rules {
        dscp RW_DSCP {
            forwarding-class CS6 {
                loss-priority low code-point DSCP-48;
            }
            forwarding-class EF {
                loss-priority low code-point DSCP-46;
            }
        }
        exp RW_EXP {
            forwarding-class CS6 {
                loss-priority low code-point 110;
            }
            forwarding-class EF {
                loss-priority low code-point 101;
            }
            forwarding-class AF4 {
                loss-priority low code-point 100;
            }
            forwarding-class AF3 {
                loss-priority low code-point 011;
            }
            forwarding-class AF2 {
                loss-priority low code-point 010;
            }
            forwarding-class AF1 {
                loss-priority low code-point 001;
            }
            forwarding-class BE {
                loss-priority low code-point 000;
            }
        }
    }
    scheduler-maps {
        SCH_MAP {
            forwarding-class CS6 scheduler S_CS6;
            forwarding-class EF scheduler S_EF;
            forwarding-class AF4 scheduler S_AF4;
            forwarding-class AF3 scheduler S_AF3;
            forwarding-class AF2 scheduler S_AF2;
            forwarding-class AF1 scheduler S_AF1;
            forwarding-class BE scheduler S_BE;
        }
    }
    schedulers {
        S_CS6 {
            transmit-rate percent 15;
            buffer-size percent 15;
            priority strict-high;
        }
        S_EF {
            transmit-rate percent 70;
            buffer-size percent 70;
            priority high;
        }
        S_AF4 {
            transmit-rate percent 5;
            buffer-size percent 5;
            priority low;
        }
        S_AF3 {
            transmit-rate percent 4;
            buffer-size percent 4;
            priority low;
        }
        S_AF2 {
            transmit-rate percent 3;
            buffer-size percent 3;
            priority low;
        }
        S_AF1 {
            transmit-rate percent 2;
            buffer-size percent 2;
            priority low;
        }
        S_BE {
            transmit-rate percent 1;
            buffer-size percent 1;
            priority low;
            drop-profile-map loss-priority any protocol any drop-profile BE_DROP_PROFILE;
        }
    }

firewall {
    family inet {
        filter 3G_CLASSIFIER {
            term SIGNAL_VOICE {
                from {
                    dscp [ 46 48 cs6 ef ];
                }
                then {
                    count CS6;
                    forwarding-class CS6;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term FINAL {
                then {
                    count EF;
                    forwarding-class EF;
                }
            }
        }
        filter 4G_Ingress {
            term 4G_VOICE {
                from {
                    dscp af42;
                }
            }
            term 4G_DEMAND {
                from {
                    dscp 18;
                }
            }
        }
        filter INTTERNET_LL_PE_2_SRT {
            interface-specific;
            term 1 {
                from {
                    source-address {
                        124.124.124.253/32;
                    }
                    destination-address {
                        123.123.123.253/32;
                    }
                }
                then {
                    count INTTERNET_LL_PE_2_SRT;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term 2 {
                then accept;
            }
        }
        filter INTTERNET_LL_SRT_2_PE {
            interface-specific;
            term 1 {
                from {
                    source-address {
                        123.123.123.253/32;
                    }
                    destination-address {
                        124.124.124.253/32;
                    }
                }
                then {
                    count INTTERNET_LL_SRT_2_PE;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term 2 {
                then accept;
            }
        }
        filter INT_DSCP_SET {
            term FINAL {
                then {
                    count INT_DSCP_SET;
                    accept;
                    dscp cs6;
                }
            }
        }
        filter CUSTOMER_A_FF {
            term INTERNET {
                from {
                    dscp cs6;
                }
                then {
                    count CUSTOMER_A_FF_INTERNET;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term DOMESTIC {
                then {
                    count CUSTOMER_A_FF_DOMESTIC;
                    accept;
                }
            }
        }
        filter TEST_POLICER {
            term final {
                then policer 100M;
            }
        }
        filter PROTECT_RE {
            interface-specific;
            term SMALL_PACKETS {
                from {
                    packet-length 0-24;
                }
                then {
                    count SMALL-PACKET-ATTACK;
                    discard;
                }
            }
            term FRAGMENT_PACKETS {
                from {
                    fragment-offset-except 0;
                    protocol [ icmp igmp pim tcp ];
                }
                then {
                    count FRAG-ATTACK;
                    discard;
                }
            }
            term TCP_DOS_PROTECTION {
                from {
                    source-prefix-list {
                        BGP_ADDRESSES;
                        LOCALHOST;
                        SSH_TELNET;
                    }
                    protocol tcp;
                    tcp-flags "(syn & !ack) | fin | rst";
                }
                then {
                    policer TCP_CONNECTION_POLICER;
                    count TCP-SYN;
                    next term;
                }
            }
            term PIM {
                from {
                    protocol pim;
                }
                then {
                    count PIM;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term BGP {
                from {
                    source-prefix-list {
                        BGP_ADDRESSES;
                        BGP_ADDRESSES_RI;
                    }
                    protocol tcp;
                    port bgp;
                }
                then {
                    count BGP;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term OSPF {
                from {
                    protocol ospf;
                }
                then {
                    count OSPF;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term DENY_LDP_DNG {
                from {
                    source-prefix-list {
                        AGG_DNG;
                    }
                    protocol [ tcp udp ];
                    port ldp;
                }
                then {
                    count DENY_LDP_DNG;
                    discard;
                }
            }
            term LDP {
                from {
                    protocol [ tcp udp ];
                    port ldp;
                }
                then {
                    count LDP;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term RSVP {
                from {
                    protocol rsvp;
                }
                then {
                    count RSVP;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term SNMP {
                from {
                    source-prefix-list {
                        SNMP;
                    }
                    protocol udp;
                    destination-port snmp;
                }
                then {
                    policer SNMP_POLICER;
                    count SNMP;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term NTP {
                from {
                    source-prefix-list {
                        NTP_SERVER_ADDRESSES;
                        NTP_LOCAL_ADDRESS;
                    }
                    destination-prefix-list {
                        NTP_LOCAL_ADDRESS;
                    }
                    protocol udp;
                    port ntp;
                }
                then {
                    policer NTP_POLICER;
                    count NTP;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term MGMT_PING {
                from {
                    source-prefix-list {
                        SSH_TELNET;
                        INTERNAL_ADDRESSES;
                        CONNECTED_ADDRESSES;
                        NMS_SERVER_RANGE;
                    }
                    protocol icmp;
                    icmp-type-except [ router-advertisement redirect ];
                }
                then {
                    policer MGMT_PING;
                    count MGMT_PING-TRAFFIC;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term PROTECT_ICMP {
                from {
                    protocol icmp;
                    icmp-type [ redirect mask-reply ];
                }
                then {
                    discard;
                }
            }
            term ICMP {
                from {
                    protocol icmp;
                    icmp-type-except [ router-advertisement redirect ];
                }
                then {
                    policer ICMP_POLICER;
                    count ICMP-TRAFFIC;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term TACACS {
                from {
                    source-prefix-list {
                        TACACPLUS_SERVER;
                    }
                    port [ tacacs tacacs-ds ];
                }
                then {
                    policer TACAC_POLICER;
                    count TACAC;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term SSH_TELNET_OUT {
                from {
                    protocol tcp;
                    source-port [ ssh telnet ];
                }
                then {
                    policer SSH_TELNET_POLICER;
                    count SSH_TELNET_OUT;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term SSH_TELNET {
                from {
                    inactive: source-prefix-list {
                        SSH_TELNET;
                    }
                    protocol tcp;
                    port [ ssh telnet ];
                }
                then {
                    policer SSH_TELNET_POLICER;
                    count SSH;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term FTP {
                from {
                    source-prefix-list {
                        SSH_TELNET;
                    }
                    protocol tcp;
                    port [ ftp ftp-data ];
                }
                then {
                    policer FTP_POLICER;
                    count FTP;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term BFD {
                from {
                    protocol udp;
                    destination-port [ 3784 4784 6784 ];
                }
                then {
                    count BFD;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term MPLS_TRACE {
                from {
                    protocol udp;
                    port 3503;
                }
                then {
                    policer ICMP_POLICER;
                    count MPLS_TRACE;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term UDP_TRACEROUTE {
                from {
                    protocol udp;
                    destination-port 33434-33523;
                }
                then {
                    policer ICMP_POLICER;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term NETCONF {
                from {
                    source-prefix-list {
                        NMS_SERVER_RANGE;
                    }
                    destination-port 830;
                }
                then {
                    policer NETCONFIG_POLICER;
                    count NETCONF-TRAFFIC;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term VRRP {
                from {
                    protocol vrrp;
                }
                then accept;
            }
            term DISCARD {
                then {
                    count DENY-TO-ROUTING-ENGINE;
                    discard;
                }
            }
        }
        filter CLEAR_DF {
            term FINAL {
                then {
                    accept;
                    dont-fragment clear;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    family vpls {
        filter COUNT_MAC {
            term BRAS {
                from {
                    source-mac-address {
                        f4:cc:55:8b:af:0f/48;
                    }
                }
                then {
                    count MAC_BRAS;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term MODEM {
                from {
                    source-mac-address {
                        78:44:76:50:61:f0/48;
                    }
                }
                then count MAC_MODEM;
            }
            term FINAL {
                then accept;
            }
        }
    }
    policer 5M {
        if-exceeding {
            bandwidth-limit 5m;
            burst-size-limit 200k;
        }
        then discard;
    }
    policer 100M {
        if-exceeding {
            bandwidth-limit 1g;
            burst-size-limit 25m;
        }
        then discard;
    }
    policer TCP_CONNECTION_POLICER {
        if-exceeding {
            bandwidth-limit 50k;
            burst-size-limit 15k;
        }
        then discard;
    }
    policer NTP_POLICER {
        if-exceeding {
            bandwidth-limit 500k;
            burst-size-limit 15k;
        }
        then discard;
    }
    policer ICMP_POLICER {
        if-exceeding {
            bandwidth-limit 5m;
            burst-size-limit 15k;
        }
        then discard;
    }
    policer SSH_TELNET_POLICER {
        if-exceeding {
            bandwidth-limit 25m;
            burst-size-limit 128k;
        }
        then discard;
    }
    policer FTP_POLICER {
        if-exceeding {
            bandwidth-limit 20m;
            burst-size-limit 625k;
        }
        then discard;
    }
    policer MGMT_PING {
        if-exceeding {
            bandwidth-limit 10m;
            burst-size-limit 100k;
        }
        then discard;
    }
    policer SNMP_POLICER {
        if-exceeding {
            bandwidth-limit 10m;
            burst-size-limit 100k;
        }
        then discard;
    }
    policer TACAC_POLICER {
        if-exceeding {
            bandwidth-limit 2m;
            burst-size-limit 100k;
        }
        then discard;
    }
    policer NETCONFIG_POLICER {
        if-exceeding {
            bandwidth-limit 5m;
            burst-size-limit 100k;
        }
        then discard;
    }
